Products with a perm rating of 0.1 and lower are considered vapor barriers.  Products with a perm rating greater than 0.1 and less than 1.0 are considered vapor retarders.  Products with a perm rating greater than 1.0 are called "breathable."  Consider ambient conditions and operating temperatures when selecting a mastic.  Consider using water-based mastics for environmental reasons.`

w:val="auto"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr><w:t>The industry does not have a clear definition that categorizes mastics into vapor barriers, vapor retarders, and breather mastics.  Specification follows the nomenclature used by Foster.  Products with a perm rating of 0.1 and lower are considered vapor barriers.  Products with a perm rating greater than 0.1 and less than 1.0 are considered vapor retarders.  Products with a perm rating greater than 1.0 are called "breathable."  Consider ambient conditions and operating temperatures when selecting a mastic.  Consider using water-based mastics for environmental reasons.</w:t></w:r></w:p><w:p w14:paraId="14FA01ED" w14:textId="77777777" w:rsidR="0053195F" w:rsidRPr="00B2779F" w:rsidRDefault="0053195F" w:rsidP="0053195F"><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="CMT"/><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:color w:val="auto"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="00B2779F"><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:color w:val="auto"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr><w:t>LEED Credit IEQ 4.1 does not address requirements for mastics.</w:t></w:r></w:p><w:p w14:paraId="5628A415" w14:textId="77777777" w:rsidR="0053195F" w:rsidRPr="00B2779F" w:rsidRDefault="0053195F" w:rsidP="0053195F"><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="PR1"/><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="00B2779F"><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr><w:t>Materials shall be compatible with insulation materials, jackets, and substrates; comply with MIL-PRF-19565C, Type II.</w:t></w:r></w:p><w:p w14:paraId="702BA24D" w14:textId="77777777" w:rsidR="0053195F" w:rsidRPr="00B2779F" w:rsidRDefault="0053195F" w:rsidP="0053195F"><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="CMT"/><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:color w:val="auto"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="00B2779F"><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="ZapfHumnst BT" w:hAnsi="ZapfHumnst BT"/><w:color w:val="auto"/><w:sz w:val="20"/></w:rPr><w:t>Retain subparagraph below if low-emitting materials are required. ### `word\endnotes.xml` - RAW XML


### `word\theme\theme1.xml` - RAW XML

### `word\webSettings.xml` - RAW XML
